},\n160\t\n161\t    /// Resume a paused worker\n162\t    Resume {\n163\t        /// Worker ID to resume, or \"all\" to resume all workers\n164\t        id: String,\n165\t    },\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\tfn            .map(|v| format!(\"v{}\", v))\n182\t                    .unwrap_or_else(|| \"previous version\".to_string());\n183\t                eprintln!(\n184\t                    \"⚠️  Update to v{} }));\n369\t}\n370\t\n371\t/// Restore terminal to its normal state.\n372\t///\n373\t/// This function is called both on normal exit and during panic handling.\n374\tfn restore_terminal() -> normalized_backend\n455\t        });\n456\t\n457\t        match found {\n458\t            Some(tool) => {\n459\t                if !tool.is_ready() {\n460\t                    eprintln!(\n461\t                        \"error: Backend '{}' is not ready: {}\",\n462\t                        backend,\n463\t                        tool.status_message()\n464\t                    );\n465\t                    if tool.status == detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey\n466\t                        && let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var\n467\t                    {\n468\t                        eprintln!(\"Set the {} environment variable and try again\", env_var);\n469\t                    }\n470\t                    return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' is not ready\", backend).into());\n471\t                }\n472\t                tool.clone()\n473\t            }\n474\t            None => {\n475\t                eprintln!(\"error: Backend '{}' not found\", backend);\n476\t         detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => {\n500\t                                // Extract missing feature from diagnostics\n501\t                                let feature = guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { missing_feature, .. } => {\n507\t                                            Some(missing_feature.clone())\n508\t                                        }\n509\t                                        _ => None,\n510\t                                    });\n511\t                                (false, true, feature)\n512\t                            }\n513\t                            _ => (false, false, None),\n514\t                        };\n515\t                        guidance::ToolFixInfo {\n516\t                            name:             }\n529\t                return Err(\"No ready tools available\".into());\n530\t            }\n531\t        }\n532\t    } else {\n533\t        // Interactive mode: show the TUI wizard for         \"\\n✨ Using: {} ({})\",\n539\t                    tool.name,\n540\t                    tool.binary_path.display()\n541\t                );\n542\t                tool\n543\t            }\n544\t            Ok(None) => {\n545\t                // User chose \"Manual Setup\" - skip auto-configuration\n546\t                eprintln!(\"\\n📝 Manual setup selected.\");\n547\t                eprintln!(\"   Create ~/.forge/config.yaml manually to configure FORGE.\");\n548\t                return Ok(());\n549\t            }\n550\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::UserCancelled) => {\n551\t                eprintln!(\"\\n👋 Setup cancelled.\");\n552\t                return Err(\"User cancelled setup\".into());\n553\t            }\n554\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::NoToolsAvailable) => {\n555\t                // This shouldn't happen since we already checked, but handle it\n556\t                eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n557\t                return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n558\t            }\n559\t            Err(e) => {\n560\t                eprintln!(\"\\nerror: Wizard failed: {}\", e);\n561\t                return Err(format!(\"Wizard failed: {}\", e).into());\n562\t            }\n563\t        }\n564\t    };\n565\t\n566\t    if selected_tool.name,\n571\t            selected_tool.binary_path.display()\n572\t        );\n573\t    }\n574\t\n575\t    // Create directory structure\n576\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n577\t generator::generate_launcher_script(&selected_tool, &launcher_path)?;\n596\t\n597\t    if !non_interactive {\n598\t        eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Configuration complete!\");\n599\t        eprintln!(\" other => other.to_string(),\n621\t    }\n622\t}\n623\t\n624\t/// Handle the `forge init` command.\n625\tfn handle_init_command(non_interactive: bool, force: bool, reconfigure: bool, detect_tools: }\n635\t\n636\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n637\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n638\t\n639\t    // Handle --reconfigure: backup existing config before re-running setup\n640\t    if reconfigure {\n641\t        if !config_path.exists() {\n642\t            if non_interactive {\n643\t                eprintln!(\"error: No configuration found to reconfigure\");\n644\t                eprintln!(\"Use 'forge init' to create initial configuration\");\n645\t            } else {\n646\t                eprintln!(\"No configuration found. Running first-time setup instead...\\n\");\n647\t            }\n648\t            // Fall through to normal setup since there's nothing to reconfigure\n649\t        } else {\n650\t            // Backup existing config before proceeding\n651\t            if let Err(e) = backup_config(&forge_dir, &config_path) {\n652\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to backup config: {}\", e);\n653\t                return ExitCode::from(1);\n654\t            }\n655\t            if !non_interactive {\n656\t                eprintln!(\"📦 Existing configuration backed up\\n\");\n657\t            }\n658\t        }\n659\t    } else if !force && config_path.exists() {\n660\t        // Neither --force nor --reconfigure: don't overwrite existing config\n661\t        if non_interactive {\n662\t            eprintln!(\n663\t                \"error: Configuration already exists at {}\",\n664\t                config_path.display()\n665\t            );\n666\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n667\t            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n668\t            return ExitCode::from(1);\n669\t        } else {\n670\t            eprintln!(\n671\t                \"Configuration already exists at {}\",\n672\t                config_path.display()\n673\t            );\n674\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n675\t            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n676\t            return ExitCode::SUCCESS;\n677\t        }\n678\t    }\n679\t\n680\t    // mode: quiet output, clear error messages to stderr\n685\t        match run_onboarding(true, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n686\t            Ok(()) => ExitCode::SUCCESS,\n687\t            Err(_) => ExitCode::from(1),\n688\t        }\n689\t    } else {\n690\t        // Interactive mode: show welcome message and full output\n691\t        eprintln!(\"🚀 FORGE Setup\");\n692\t        eprintln!();\n693\t\n694\t        match run_onboarding(false, preferred_backend.as_deref()) {\n695\t            Ok(()) => {\n696\t                eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Setup complete!\");\n697\t                ExitCode::SUCCESS\n698\t            }\n699\t            Err(e) => {\n700\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Setup failed: {}\", e);\n701\t                ExitCode::from(1)\n702\t            }\n703\t        }\n704\t    }\n705\t}\n706\t\n707\t/// Backup existing config.yaml before reconfiguration.\n708\t///\n709\t/// Creates a timestamped backup to preserve user's previous settings.\n710\t/// Keeps logs, costs database, and status files intact.\n711\tfn backup_config(forge_dir: &std::path::Path, config_path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<std::path::PathBuf, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n712\t    let timestamp = chrono::Local::now().format(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\");\n713\t    let backup_path = forge_dir.join(format!(\"config.yaml.backup.{}\", timestamp));\n714\t\n715\t    std::fs::copy(config_path,    if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n728\t                    && (content.contains(\"# CUSTOM:\") || content.contains(\"# USER:\") || content.contains(\"# Modified by\")) {\n729\t                        eprintln!(\"⚠️  Warning: {} may contain custom modifications\", path.display());\n730\t                        // Backup the launcher script too\n731\t                        let    }\n741\t\n742\t    Ok(backup_path)\n743\t}\n744\t\n745\t/// Handle the `forge init --detect-tools` command.\n746\t///\n747\t/// Runs CLI tool detection and displays results without modifying any      ExitCode::from(1)\n827\t        }\n828\t    }\n829\t}\n830\t\n831\t/// Validate the config file and offer recovery if invalid.\n832\tfn validate_config() -> Result<(), String> {\n833\t    use eprintln!();\n883\t                    Ok(())\n884\t                }\n885\t                \"3\" | \"\" => {\n886\t                    Err(\"Exiting. collaboration.\n1143\tfn run_server_mode(bind_address: String, port: u16) -> ExitCode {\n1144\t    use forge_tui::{ClientConfig, App};\n1145\t\n1146\t    info!(\"Starting FORGE in server mode on WebSocket for multi-user collaboration.\n    ///\n    /// # Arguments\n    ///\n    /// * `config` - Client configuration with server URL and credentials\n    pub fn run_with_client(config: ClientConfig) -> AppResult<()> {\n        use std::sync::mpsc::{self, Receiver, Sender, TryRecvError};\n        use tokio::runtime::Runtime;\n\n        info!(\"Starting FORGE in client mode, connecting to {}\", config.server_url);\n\n        // Create tokio runtime for async WebSocket client\n        let rt = Runtime::new()\n            .map_err(|e| Box::new(std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::Other, e)))?;\n\n        // Create channels for communication with the background client task\n        let (request_tx, request_rx) =
